@name 
@inputs EGP:wirelink
@outputs 
@persist HTML:string Title:string Style:array
@trigger 

if (first()) {
    function displayHTML(Html:string) {
        local Index = 1
        local YPos = 20  #   Y

        #  <title>
        if (Html:find("<title>") & Html:find("</title>")) {
            local Start = Html:find("<title>") + 7
            local End = Html:find("</title>")
            Title = Html:sub(Start, End - 1)
            EGP:egpText(Index, Title, vec2(200, YPos))  #  
            EGP:egpColor(Index, vec(255, 255, 0))  #  
            YPos += 40  #   Y
            Index += 1
            Html = Html:replace("<title>" + Title + "</title>", "")  #   
        }

        #  <style>
        if (Html:find("<style>") & Html:find("</style>")) {
            local Start = Html:find("<style>") + 7
            local End = Html:find("</style>")
            local StyleContent = Html:sub(Start, End - 1)
            # :      'h1 { color: 255,0,0; }'
            if (StyleContent:find("h1")) {
                local ColorStart = StyleContent:find("color:") + 6
                local ColorEnd = StyleContent:find(";")
                local ColorValues = StyleContent:sub(ColorStart, ColorEnd - 1):explode(",")
                Style[Index,vector] = vec(ColorValues[1,string]:toNumber(), ColorValues[2,string]:toNumber(), ColorValues[3,string]:toNumber())  #    <h1>
            }
            Html = Html:replace("<style>" + StyleContent + "</style>", "")  #  
        }

        #  <h1>
        while (Html:find("<h1>") & Html:find("</h1>")) {
            local Start = Html:find("<h1>") + 4
            local End = Html:find("</h1>")
            local Content = Html:sub(Start,End - 1)
            EGP:egpText(Index, Content, vec2(200, YPos))  #  
            #      <h1>   Style
            local Color = Style[Index,vector]  
            EGP:egpColor(Index, Color)  #   
            YPos += 40  #   Y
            Index += 1
            Html = Html:replace("<h1>" + Content + "</h1>", "")  #   
        }

        #         
    }

    #  HTML  
    HTML =
